Creating a `DataSplitter` object with overhead\n2. Creating a new Series object for each group (manager creation, axes setup)\n3. Python-level iteration without cache locality optimization\n4. No exploitation of data locality\n\n## Solution\nImplemented `_aggregate_series_fast` with the following optimizations:\n\n### Key Optimizations\n\n1. **Cache Locality (Data Sorting)**\n   - Uses `get_group_index_sorter()` to pre-sort data by group index\n   - All data for the same group becomes contiguous in memory\n   - Improves CPU cache hit rate significantly\n\n2. **Efficient Group Boundary Detection**\n   - Uses `lib.generate_slices()` to find group start/end indices\n   - Avoids creating DataSplitter objects\n   - Direct calculation of group boundaries\n\n3. **Reduced Series Object Overhead**\n   - Uses `.iloc[]` slicing instead of full Series reconstruction\n   - Minimizes manager creation overhead\n   - Direct array access for each group slice\n\n4. **Intelligent Fast Path Selection**\n   - Checks preconditions before using fast path:\n     - Non-empty Series (len(obj) > 0)\n     - ngroups > 0\n     - Single index (not MultiIndex)\n     - NumPy array backed (not ExtensionArray)\n   - Falls back to pure Python for unsupported cases\n   - Proper error handling with try-except\n\n## Performance Impact\n\nThe optimization targets:\n- Reduction in object creation overhead\n- Better cache locality through data sorting\n- Faster group boundary calculation\n- More direct array access patterns\n\nFor large datasets with many groups, this should provide significant speedup over the pure Python version.\n\n## Implementation Details\n\nThe `_aggregate_series_fast` method:\n1. Gets sorted indices using `get_group_index_sorter()`\n2. Pre-sorts data and labels for cache locality\n3. Uses `lib.generate_slices()` to find group boundaries\n4. Iterates through groups with direct index-based slicing\n5. Applies aggregation function to each group slice\n6. Stores results in pre-allocated array\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\n- Maintains the same interface as before\n- Falls back to pure Python on error\n- All existing functionality preserved\n- Tests should pass unchanged\n- Performance-transparent to users (they get faster results)\n\n## Files Modified\n\n- `pandas/core/groupby/ops.py`: Added `_aggregate_series_fast()` method and updated `agg_series()` to use it\nEOF\n\ncat /workspace/OPTIMIZATION_SUMMARY.md\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":526,"cache_read_input_tokens":92335,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":526},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"45d740fc-1a37-4922-954e-33035a1dfa29","uuid":"493aba68-e630-47a1-a908-15d079dc0aed"}
